For example, the replace operations can be used to get the same result of adding or removing (replace something with extra or empty).\r\n\r\n- The program tries to make the most sense for file naming and renaming. For example, title-case operation will change to upper-case all the characters immediately after the period (.), dash (-), underscore (_), and whitespace characters. If that’s not you want, then replace operations can get what you want.\r\n\r\n- Naming collision: there are cases, for example, you select a file to rename and that new name would be the same with an existing one in the same location, or a new file has been moved into the same location before the execution of the program. Please note that the preview in this case doesn’t show the result you will get as it depends on what things are at runtime.\r\n\r\nExample for this case might be, assume that you have three files with names: ‘World.txt’, ‘Hello_World.txt’, and ‘Hello_Neighbor.txt’. Then it comes back working with that unique temporary name, and determine whether to leave as that name currently is, or change to your desired name.\r\n\r\nThis explanation might seem lengthy and complicated, but the case is not common, but also can happen so it needs to be mentioned. The abort operation can result in that unique naming, so don’t abort if you don’t really need to. Just wait for the program to finish its job.\r\n\r\n- Undo: you can undo only one-step backward (the immediate last change). The number of filenames that has been changed is re-counted at each change, or when the program starts. Un serveur VPN auquel vous vous connectez, par exemple via le VPN Hotspot Shield, établit une connexion chiffrée, et sécurisée, à un serveur situé dans un autre pays. Grâce à ce chiffrement, les données transmises ne peuvent être ni filtrées ni bloquées. \r\n\r\n* Pourquoi utiliser un VPN ?\r\nUn VPN ne permet pas seulement d'accéder à des services censurés ou bloqués, comme Facebook, Pandora ou YouTube, mais vous bénéficiez également d'une sécurité et d'une confidentialité en ligne optimales. Vous pouvez surfer sur le web anonymement et en toute sécurité.\r\n\r\n* Comparaison VPN / Proxy\r\nUn VPN et un proxy peuvent tous deux empêcher votre identification en redirigeant votre trafic internet et en modifiant votre adresse IP. À l'inverse, un service VPN chiffre tout votre trafic et fonctionne avec tous les services basés sur internet.
